     1	"""Nondimensionalization helpers for Butler-Volmer BV parameters."""
     2	
     3	from __future__ import annotations
     4	
     5	from Nondim.constants import FARADAY_CONSTANT, GAS_CONSTANT
     6	
     7	
     8	def _add_bv_scaling_to_transform(
     9	    scaling: dict,
    10	    bv_cfg: dict,
    11	    *,
    12	    n_species: int,
    13	    nondim_enabled: bool,
    14	    kappa_inputs_dimless: bool,
    15	    concentration_inputs_dimless: bool = False,
    16	) -> dict:
    17	    """Augment the ModelScaling dict with BV-specific nondimensional quantities.
    18	
    19	    Returns a new dict (does not mutate scaling).
    20	
    21	    Parameters
    22	    ----------
    23	    concentration_inputs_dimless:
    24	        If True, ``bv_bc.c_ref`` values are already dimensionless (divided by the
    25	        concentration scale) and must NOT be scaled again.  If False (default),
    26	        c_ref values are in physical units (mol/m³) and will be divided by
    27	        ``concentration_scale_mol_m3``.  Mirror of ``kappa_inputs_dimless``.
    28	    """
    29	    kappa_scale = scaling.get("kappa_scale_m_s", 1.0)
    30	    thermal_voltage_v = scaling.get("thermal_voltage_v", 0.02569)
    31	    conc_scale = scaling.get("concentration_scale_mol_m3", 1.0)
    32	    potential_scale = scaling.get("potential_scale_v", 1.0)
    33	
    34	    k0_raw = bv_cfg["k0_vals"]
    35	    c_ref_raw = bv_cfg["c_ref_vals"]
    36	    E_eq_raw = bv_cfg["E_eq_v"]
    37	
    38	    if not nondim_enabled:
    39	        # Dimensional: keep physical values, apply F/(RT) as EM prefactor for exponents
    40	        k0_model = k0_raw
    41	        c_ref_model = c_ref_raw
    42	        # Exponent in BV: exp(±α · F · η / RT).  In dimensional mode phi is in Volts.
    43	        # The BV exponent prefactor = F/(RT).
    44	        bv_exponent_scale = FARADAY_CONSTANT / (GAS_CONSTANT * scaling["temperature_k"])
    45	        E_eq_model = E_eq_raw
    46	    else:
    47	        # Nondimensional: k0 → k0/κ_scale, c_ref → c_ref/c_scale
    48	        # Exponent: exp(±α · η̂) where η̂ = η/V_T (dimensionless potential already)
    49	        # Since potential is already in V_T units, exponent prefactor = 1.
    50	        bv_exponent_scale = 1.0
    51	        if kappa_inputs_dimless:
    52	            k0_model = k0_raw  # already dimensionless
    53	        else:
    54	            k0_model = [v / kappa_scale for v in k0_raw]
    55	        if concentration_inputs_dimless:
    56	            c_ref_model = c_ref_raw  # already dimensionless, do not divide by c_scale
    57	        else:
    58	            c_ref_model = [v / conc_scale for v in c_ref_raw]
    59	        # E_eq in thermal voltage units
    60	        E_eq_model = E_eq_raw / potential_scale
    61	
    62	    # Stern layer capacitance nondimensionalization.
    63	    # Physical BC: epsilon * grad(phi).n = C_stern * (phi_m - phi)
    64	    #
    65	    # In the weak form, the IBP boundary integral is eps_coeff * grad(phi_hat).n.
    66	    # The Stern BC replaces this, so the weak-form coefficient must satisfy:
    67	    #   stern_model * (phi_m_hat - phi_hat) = eps_coeff * grad(phi_hat).n
    68	    #   = eps_coeff * (C_stern * L / epsilon) * (phi_m_hat - phi_hat)
    69	    #
    70	    # In dimensional mode:
    71	    #   eps_coeff = permittivity, boundary integral = permittivity * grad(phi).n
    72	    #   Physical BC: permittivity * grad(phi).n = C_stern * (phi_m - phi)
    73	    #   stern_model = C_stern  (direct physical value, used without eps_coeff)
    74	    #
    75	    # In nondim mode:
    76	    #   eps_coeff = epsilon * V_T / (F * c_ref * L^2)
    77	    #   stern_model = eps_coeff * C_stern * L / epsilon
    78	    #              = C_stern * V_T / (F * c_ref * L)  [dimensionless]
    79	    stern_raw = bv_cfg.get("stern_capacitance_f_m2")
    80	    if stern_raw is not None and float(stern_raw) > 0:
    81	        if not nondim_enabled:
    82	            stern_model = float(stern_raw)
    83	        else:
    84	            length_scale = scaling.get("length_scale_m", 1.0)
    85	            concentration_scale = scaling.get("concentration_scale_mol_m3", 1.0)
    86	            stern_model = (
    87	                float(stern_raw) * potential_scale
    88	                / (FARADAY_CONSTANT * concentration_scale * length_scale)
    89	            )
    90	    else:
    91	        stern_model = None
    92	
    93	    out = dict(scaling)
    94	    out["bv_k0_model_vals"] = k0_model
    95	    out["bv_c_ref_model_vals"] = c_ref_model
    96	    out["bv_exponent_scale"] = bv_exponent_scale
    97	    out["bv_E_eq_model"] = E_eq_model
    98	    out["bv_alpha_vals"] = bv_cfg["alpha_vals"]
    99	    out["bv_stoichiometry"] = bv_cfg["stoichiometry"]
   100	    out["bv_stern_capacitance_model"] = stern_model
   101	    return out
   102	
   103	
   104	def _add_bv_reactions_scaling_to_transform(
   105	    scaling: dict,
   106	    reactions: list[dict],
   107	    *,
   108	    nondim_enabled: bool,
   109	    kappa_inputs_dimless: bool,
   110	    concentration_inputs_dimless: bool = False,
   111	    E_eq_v: float = 0.0,
   112	) -> dict:
   113	    """Augment ModelScaling with multi-reaction BV quantities.
   114	
   115	    Each reaction's k0 and c_ref are nondimensionalized individually.
   116	    """
   117	    kappa_scale = scaling.get("kappa_scale_m_s", 1.0)
   118	    conc_scale = scaling.get("concentration_scale_mol_m3", 1.0)
   119	    potential_scale = scaling.get("potential_scale_v", 1.0)
   120	
   121	    if not nondim_enabled:
   122	        bv_exponent_scale = FARADAY_CONSTANT / (GAS_CONSTANT * scaling["temperature_k"])
   123	        E_eq_model = E_eq_v
   124	    else:
   125	        bv_exponent_scale = 1.0
   126	        E_eq_model = E_eq_v / potential_scale
   127	
   128	    scaled_reactions = []
   129	    for rxn in reactions:
   130	        srxn = dict(rxn)
   131	        if not nondim_enabled:
   132	            srxn["k0_model"] = rxn["k0"]
   133	            srxn["c_ref_model"] = rxn["c_ref"]
   134	            srxn["E_eq_model"] = rxn.get("E_eq_v", 0.0)
   135	        else:
   136	            if kappa_inputs_dimless:
   137	                srxn["k0_model"] = rxn["k0"]
   138	            else:
   139	                srxn["k0_model"] = rxn["k0"] / kappa_scale
   140	            if concentration_inputs_dimless:
   141	                srxn["c_ref_model"] = rxn["c_ref"]
   142	            else:
   143	                srxn["c_ref_model"] = rxn["c_ref"] / conc_scale
   144	            srxn["E_eq_model"] = rxn.get("E_eq_v", 0.0) / potential_scale
   145	
   146	        # Scale cathodic_conc_factors c_ref_nondim values
   147	        scaled_factors = []
   148	        for f_cfg in rxn.get("cathodic_conc_factors", []):
   149	            sf = dict(f_cfg)
   150	            if nondim_enabled and not concentration_inputs_dimless:
   151	                sf["c_ref_nondim"] = f_cfg["c_ref_nondim"] / conc_scale
   152	            else:
   153	                sf["c_ref_nondim"] = f_cfg["c_ref_nondim"]
   154	            scaled_factors.append(sf)
   155	        srxn["cathodic_conc_factors"] = scaled_factors
   156	
   157	        scaled_reactions.append(srxn)
   158	
   159	    # Stern layer capacitance is not set via the reactions path directly;
   160	    # it comes from the bv_cfg which is handled by build_forms.  Store None
   161	    # so downstream code can check uniformly.
   162	    out = dict(scaling)
   163	    out["bv_reactions"] = scaled_reactions
   164	    out["bv_exponent_scale"] = bv_exponent_scale
   165	    out["bv_E_eq_model"] = E_eq_model
   166	    if "bv_stern_capacitance_model" not in out:
   167	        out["bv_stern_capacitance_model"] = None
   168	    return out

   304	        ``Forward.bv_solver`` uses.
   305	    """
   306	    cfg: Dict[str, Any] = {
   307	        "clip_exponent": True,
   308	        # exponent_clip = 100.0 is the only PC-trustworthy setting:
   309	        # at clip=50 (production until 2026-05-04) PC is fictitious
   310	        # below V_RHE = -0.1 V (sign-flipped, 3-4 OOM off; CD is OK).
   311	        # Do not lower this for forward runs whose PC will be compared
   312	        # against experiment.  See docs/clipping_conventions.md.
   313	        "exponent_clip": 100.0,
   314	        "regularize_concentration": True,
   315	        "conc_floor": 1e-12,
   316	        "use_eta_in_bv": True,
   317	        "bv_log_rate": log_rate,
   318	        "u_clamp": u_clamp,
   319	        "formulation": str(formulation).strip().lower(),
   320	        "initializer": str(initializer).strip().lower(),
   321	    }
   322	    if softplus:
   323	        cfg["softplus_regularization"] = True
   324	    return cfg
   325	
   326	
   327	def _make_nondim_cfg() -> Dict[str, Any]:
   328	    """Standard nondimensionalization config sub-dict."""
   329	    return {
   330	        "enabled": True,
   331	        "diffusivity_scale_m2_s": D_REF,
   332	        "concentration_scale_mol_m3": C_SCALE,
   333	        "length_scale_m": L_REF,
   334	        "potential_scale_v": V_T,
   335	        "kappa_scale_m_s": K_SCALE,
   336	        "time_scale_s": L_REF**2 / D_REF,
   337	        "kappa_inputs_are_dimensionless": True,
   338	        "diffusivity_inputs_are_dimensionless": True,
   339	        "concentration_inputs_are_dimensionless": True,
   340	        "potential_inputs_are_dimensionless": True,
   341	        "time_inputs_are_dimensionless": True,
   342	    }
   343	
   344	
   345	def _make_bv_bc_cfg(
   346	    species: SpeciesConfig,
   347	    *,
   348	    k0_hat_r1: float = K0_HAT_R1,
   349	    k0_hat_r2: float = K0_HAT_R2,
   350	    alpha_r1: float = ALPHA_R1,
   351	    alpha_r2: float = ALPHA_R2,
   352	    E_eq_r1: float = E_EQ_R1_V,
   353	    E_eq_r2: float = E_EQ_R2_V,
   354	    c_hp_hat: float = C_HP_HAT,
   355	    electrode_marker: int = 3,
   356	    concentration_marker: int = 4,
   357	    ground_marker: int = 4,
   358	    boltzmann_counterions: Optional[Sequence[Dict[str, Any]]] = None,
   359	    stern_capacitance_f_m2: Optional[float] = None,
   360	    include_h_factor: Optional[bool] = None,
   361	    bv_reactions: Optional[Sequence[Dict[str, Any]]] = None,
   362	) -> Dict[str, Any]:
   363	    """Build the ``bv_bc`` config sub-dict for 2-reaction BV.
   364	
   365	    Parameters
   366	    ----------
   367	    boltzmann_counterions:
   368	        Optional list of analytic-Boltzmann counterion entries for Poisson
   369	        (Poisson-Boltzmann-Nernst-Planck reduction).  Each entry is a dict
   370	        with keys ``z`` and ``c_bulk_nondim``.  When provided, the forms
   371	        modules add a residual ``-charge_rhs * z * c_bulk * exp(-z*phi)``
   372	        per entry to Poisson's equation.  See
   373	        ``Forward/bv_solver/boltzmann.py``.
   374	    stern_capacitance_f_m2:
   375	        Optional compact-layer Stern capacitance in physical units
   376	        ``F/m²`` (1 F/m² = 100 µF/cm²).  When ``None`` the cfg key is
   377	        omitted entirely and the no-Stern Dirichlet BC ``phi_s = phi_m``
   378	        is used (the idealised C_S → ∞ limit).  When set to a positive
   379	        value, ``forms_logc.py`` switches to a Robin BC that lets the
   380	        compact-layer voltage drop ``phi_m - phi_s`` be solved for, and
   381	        the BV overpotential becomes ``eta = phi_applied - phi - E_eq``.
   382	        A value of ``0.0`` is written through but is runtime-inactive
   383	        (``forms_logc.py`` requires ``> 0`` to activate Stern).
   384	    include_h_factor:
   385	        Whether to attach H+ stoichiometric concentration factors to each
   386	        reaction's ``cathodic_conc_factors``.  Defaults to True for
   387	        ``species.n_species >= 3`` (works for both the 4sp charged preset
   388	        and the 3sp logc+Boltzmann preset).
   389	    bv_reactions:
   390	        Optional list of fully-specified reaction dicts.  When set, takes
   391	        precedence over the legacy ``k0_hat_r{1,2}, alpha_r{1,2},
   392	        E_eq_r{1,2}`` keyword bundle and the species ``stoichiometry_r{1,2}``
   393	        fields — the BV residual loop iterates over this list directly.
   394	        Each entry must provide ``k0`` (nondim), ``alpha``, ``n_electrons``,
   395	        ``E_eq_v`` (V vs RHE), ``cathodic_species``, ``anodic_species``
   396	        (or None), ``stoichiometry`` (per-species int list of length
   397	        ``n_species``), ``c_ref``, ``reversible``, and optionally
   398	        ``cathodic_conc_factors``.  Used by the parallel-2e/4e topology
   399	        (M3a.2, 2026-05-07) to bypass the hardcoded sequential R_1/R_2
   400	        construction; see ``PARALLEL_2E_4E_REACTIONS`` below.
   401	    """
   402	    if bv_reactions is not None:
   403	        # Caller-supplied reactions list takes precedence over the legacy
   404	        # R_1/R_2 keyword construction.  Deep-copy each entry so internal
   405	        # mutation (e.g. nondimensionalization in
   406	        # ``_add_bv_reactions_scaling_to_transform``) does not leak
   407	        # back to the caller's literal.
   408	        reactions_out = []
   409	        for rxn in bv_reactions:
   410	            rxn_copy = dict(rxn)
   411	            # Deep-copy nested factor lists so they cannot share state.
   412	            if "cathodic_conc_factors" in rxn_copy and rxn_copy["cathodic_conc_factors"]:
   413	                rxn_copy["cathodic_conc_factors"] = [
   414	                    dict(f) for f in rxn_copy["cathodic_conc_factors"]
   415	                ]
   416	            if "stoichiometry" in rxn_copy:
   417	                rxn_copy["stoichiometry"] = list(rxn_copy["stoichiometry"])
   418	            reactions_out.append(rxn_copy)
   419	    else:
   420	        reaction_1: Dict[str, Any] = {
   421	            "k0": k0_hat_r1,
   422	            "alpha": alpha_r1,
   423	            "cathodic_species": 0,
   424	            "anodic_species": 1,
   425	            "c_ref": 1.0,
   426	            "stoichiometry": list(species.stoichiometry_r1),
   427	            "n_electrons": N_ELECTRONS,
   428	            "reversible": True,
   429	            "E_eq_v": E_eq_r1,
   430	        }
   431	        reaction_2: Dict[str, Any] = {
   432	            "k0": k0_hat_r2,
   433	            "alpha": alpha_r2,
   434	            "cathodic_species": 1,
   435	            "anodic_species": None,
   436	            "c_ref": 0.0,
   437	            "stoichiometry": list(species.stoichiometry_r2),
   438	            "n_electrons": N_ELECTRONS,
   439	            "reversible": False,
   440	            "E_eq_v": E_eq_r2,
   441	        }
   442	
   443	        # H+ stoichiometric concentration factor.  Apply automatically when the
   444	        # species set has at least 3 species (i.e. tracks H+ explicitly), unless
   445	        # the caller overrides via include_h_factor.
   446	        if include_h_factor is None:
   447	            attach_h = species.n_species >= 3
   448	        else:
   449	            attach_h = bool(include_h_factor)
   450	        if attach_h:
   451	            h_factor = [{"species": 2, "power": 2, "c_ref_nondim": c_hp_hat}]
   452	            reaction_1["cathodic_conc_factors"] = h_factor
   453	            reaction_2["cathodic_conc_factors"] = [dict(f) for f in h_factor]
   454	
   455	        reactions_out = [reaction_1, reaction_2]
   456	
   457	    cfg: Dict[str, Any] = {
   458	        "reactions": reactions_out,
   459	        # Legacy per-species fallback (used by _get_bv_cfg for markers)
   460	        "k0": list(species.k0_legacy),
   461	        "alpha": list(species.alpha_legacy),
   462	        "stoichiometry": list(species.stoichiometry_legacy),
   463	        "c_ref": list(species.c_ref_legacy),
   464	        "E_eq_v": 0.0,
   465	        "electrode_marker": electrode_marker,
   466	        "concentration_marker": concentration_marker,
   467	        "ground_marker": ground_marker,
   468	    }
   469	    if boltzmann_counterions:
   470	        cfg["boltzmann_counterions"] = [dict(entry) for entry in boltzmann_counterions]

     1	"""Hybrid proton-electrochemical-potential transform for the BV PNP solver.
     2	
     3	Experimental ``formulation="logc_muh"`` formulation.  Mirrors
     4	``forms_logc.py`` but stores the proton (H+) primary variable as the
     5	electrochemical potential
     6	
     7	    mu_H = u_H + em * z_H * phi    where    em*z_H = +1 in the production scaling
     8	
     9	so that ``c_H = exp(mu_H - em*z_H*phi)`` is reconstructed from the muh
    10	unknown plus the resolved phi.  In Debye/Boltzmann regions ``mu_H`` is
    11	nearly flat (``log(c_H_bulk)``), even when ``u_H`` and ``phi`` each vary
    12	by tens of log-units, giving Newton a much smoother primary variable.
    13	The Nernst-Planck flux for the muh species reduces to
    14	
    15	    J_H = -D_H * c_H * grad(mu_H)
    16	
    17	with no separate ``em*z*grad(phi)`` drift term.
    18	
    19	Non-mu species (O2, H2O2 — neutrals) are unchanged from ``forms_logc.py``:
    20	their primary variables remain ``u_i = log(c_i)``.
    21	
    22	This module is a near-clone of ``forms_logc.py`` with substitutions on the
    23	five ``c_H``-touch sites (NP flux, BV surface concentration, BV log-rate,
    24	Bikerman packing, Poisson source) plus the IC pair.  The duplication is
    25	intentional for the experimental phase; consolidation is tracked for after
    26	Phase 7 (charged-species mu) lands.
    27	
    28	Critical implementation notes:
    29	
    30	* ``c_H_old`` for the time term must reconstruct using ``phi_prev =
    31	  U_prev.sub(n)``, not the current ``phi``.  Otherwise the time
    32	  derivative is silently wrong on transient runs.
    33	* The ``u_clamp`` is applied to the reconstructed ``log(c_H) = mu_H -
    34	  em*z_H*phi``, NOT to the raw ``mu_H``.  Raw ``mu_H`` is offset by
    35	  ``phi`` (O(40) at high V), so a symmetric clamp on raw mu_H imposes a
    36	  different physical bound than for ``forms_logc``.
    37	* The ``debye_boltzmann`` IC for muh exhibits an analytic cancellation:
    38	  with ``em*z_H = 1``, ``mu_H_init = u_H_init + em*z_H*phi_init =
    39	  log(H_outer) - psi + log(H_outer/c_clo4_bulk) + psi = 2*log(H_outer) -
    40	  log(c_clo4_bulk)``.  The diffuse-layer ``psi`` cancels exactly --
    41	  Boltzmann equilibrium -> mu_H is smooth in y.
    42	
    43	See:
    44	
    45	* ``docs/electrochemical_potential_solver_plan.md`` (scoping doc and
    46	  multi-phase landing plan with traps + sequencing).
    47	* ``docs/PNP_BV_Analytical_Simplifications.md`` -- the rigorous reason
    48	  ``mu_i`` is the smooth variable in the Debye layer.
    49	* ``docs/4sp_bikerman_ic_option_2b_results.md`` -- the May 4 sweep
    50	  exercising this backend end-to-end on the production target stack.
    51	"""
    52	
    53	from __future__ import annotations
    54	
    55	from typing import Any
    56	
    57	import math
    58	import numpy as np
    59	import firedrake as fd
    60	
    61	from Nondim.transform import build_model_scaling, _get_nondim_cfg, _bool

    67	    _get_bv_boltzmann_counterions_cfg,
    68	)

    70	from .boltzmann import (
    71	    add_boltzmann_counterion_residual,
    72	    build_steric_boltzmann_expressions,
    73	)
    74	from .forms_logc import build_context_logc, set_initial_conditions_logc
    75	
    76	
    77	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    78	# Helpers
    79	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    80	
    81	def _resolve_mu_h_index(z_vals: list) -> int:
    82	    """Return the index of the proton species (z = +1) for the muh formulation.
    83	
    84	    Phase 2 of the muh landing is *hybrid* -- only H+ becomes the mu
    85	    variable; ClO4- (z = -1, when dynamic) stays as u-log-c.  Charged-species
    86	    mu for 4sp+Bikerman is Phase 7 and lives in a separate forms file.
    87	    """
    88	    candidates = [i for i, zv in enumerate(z_vals) if abs(float(zv) - 1.0) < 1e-12]
    89	    if not candidates:
    90	        raise ValueError(
    91	            "formulation='logc_muh' requires a species with z=+1 (H+); none found "
    92	            f"in z_vals={list(z_vals)}."
    93	        )
    94	    if len(candidates) > 1:
    95	        raise ValueError(
    96	            "formulation='logc_muh' requires exactly one species with z=+1 (H+); "
    97	            f"found {len(candidates)} (indices {candidates})."
    98	        )
    99	    return candidates[0]
   100	
   101	
   102	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   103	# Public API
   104	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   105	
   106	def build_context_logc_muh(solver_params: Any, *, mesh: Any = None) -> dict[str, Any]:
   107	    """Build mesh and function spaces for muh BV PNP solver.
   108	
   109	    Identical mixed-space layout to ``build_context_logc`` -- the muh
   110	    transform changes only the *interpretation* of ``U.sub(mu_h_idx)``, not
   111	    the function space.  Marks the context with ``logc_muh_transform=True``
   112	    so downstream diagnostics know to read concentrations through
   113	    ``ctx['ci_exprs']`` rather than ``np.exp(U.sub(i).dat...)``.
   114	    """
   115	    ctx = build_context_logc(solver_params, mesh=mesh)
   116	    ctx["logc_muh_transform"] = True
   117	    return ctx

   831	    poisson_coefficient = float(scaling.get("poisson_coefficient", 1.0))
   832	    lambda_D = math.sqrt(max(poisson_coefficient, 1e-300))
   833	    em = float(scaling.get("electromigration_prefactor", 1.0))
   834	
   835	    z_vals_full = list(solver_params[4])
   836	    mu_h_idx = _resolve_mu_h_index(z_vals_full[:n])
   837	    z_h_val = float(z_vals_full[mu_h_idx])
   838	
   839	    D_model_vals = [float(v) for v in scaling.get("D_model_vals", [1.0] * n)]
   840	    if np.isscalar(c0):
   841	        c0_raw = [float(c0)] * n
   842	    else:
   843	        c0_raw = [float(v) for v in list(c0)][:n]
   844	    c0_model = [max(float(v), 1e-300) for v in scaling.get("c0_model_vals", c0_raw)]
   845	
   846	    # ----- Locate the Boltzmann counterion bulk concentration ---------
   847	    counterions = _get_bv_boltzmann_counterions_cfg(params)
   848	    synthesised_4sp_counterion = False
   849	    if not counterions:
   850	        if (
   851	            n == 4
   852	            and len(z_vals_full) >= 4
   853	            and int(z_vals_full[3]) == -1
   854	            and len(c0_model) >= 4
   855	        ):
   856	            counterions = [{
   857	                "z": -1,
   858	                "c_bulk_nondim": float(c0_model[3]),
   859	            }]
   860	            synthesised_4sp_counterion = True
   861	    if not counterions:
   862	        return False, "no_boltzmann_counterion", 0
   863	
   864	    # Phase 2 hybrid muh -- proton at index 2 (production 3sp+Boltzmann)
   865	    # and matched-asymptotic Picard layout (O2, H2O2, H+ at indices
   866	    # 0, 1, 2) is required.  Reject configurations where mu_h_idx != 2,
   867	    # or fall through to logc IC.  The orchestrator's fallback handles
   868	    # this gracefully.
   869	    if mu_h_idx != 2:
   870	        return False, f"mu_h_idx_unsupported ({mu_h_idx} != 2)", 0
   871	
   872	    O_b = c0_model[0]
   873	    P_b = c0_model[1]
   874	    H_b = c0_model[2]
   875	    D_O = max(D_model_vals[0], 1e-30)
   876	    D_P = max(D_model_vals[1], 1e-30)
   877	    D_H = max(D_model_vals[2], 1e-30)
   878	    # P_FLOOR: 1e-30 (numerical floor only).  See forms_logc.py
   879	    # counterpart for the rate-consistency rationale.
   880	    P_FLOOR = 1e-30
   881	
   882	    c_clo4_bulk = max(float(counterions[0]["c_bulk_nondim"]), 1e-300)
   883	
   884	    bv_exp_scale = float(scaling.get("bv_exponent_scale", 1.0))
   885	    exponent_clip = float(conv_cfg.get("exponent_clip", 100.0))
   886	    clip_exponent = bool(conv_cfg.get("clip_exponent", True))
   887	
   888	    # Per-reaction scalars are read directly from ``bv_reactions`` by
   889	    # ``picard_outer_loop_general``; M3a.2 unpacking removed (per v3
   890	    # §9 contract item 2).  See ``forms_logc.py`` counterpart.
   891	
   892	    # Two paths reach the bikerman-consistent IC.
   893	    bikerman_in_counterions = bool(counterions) and any(
   894	        e.get("steric_mode", "ideal") == "bikerman" for e in counterions
   895	    )
   896	    apply_bikerman_ic = synthesised_4sp_counterion or bikerman_in_counterions
   897	
   898	    # Bikerman size parameters for the Picard's surface gamma; same
   899	    # branching as forms_logc.py.  ``a_h = a_cl = 0`` -> legacy
   900	    # gamma-free Picard.
   901	    if apply_bikerman_ic:
   902	        a_vals_full_for_picard = list(solver_params[6])
   903	        a_h_picard = float(a_vals_full_for_picard[2])
   904	        if synthesised_4sp_counterion:
   905	            a_cl_picard = float(a_vals_full_for_picard[3])
   906	            c_cl_anchor_kind = "synthesised_4sp"
   907	        else:
   908	            bikerman_entry_for_picard = next(
   909	                e for e in counterions
   910	                if e.get("steric_mode", "ideal") == "bikerman"
   911	            )
   912	            a_cl_picard = float(bikerman_entry_for_picard["a_nondim"])
   913	            c_cl_anchor_kind = "bulk"
   914	    else:
   915	        a_h_picard = 0.0
   916	        a_cl_picard = 0.0
   917	        c_cl_anchor_kind = "bulk"
   918	
   919	    # Stern split (Bug #1 fix); see forms_logc.py counterpart for the
   920	    # rationale.  The post-Stern psi_D returned by picard_outer_loop
   921	    # automatically gets picked up by the BKSA composite-psi profile,
   922	    # so phi(y=0) = phi_applied - psi_S after IC interpolation.  The
   923	    # muh formulation's mu_h_init = u_h_init + em*z_H*phi_init inherits
   924	    # the shift via phi_init (psi cancellation algebra still holds).
   925	    stern_capacitance_model = scaling.get("bv_stern_capacitance_model")
   926	    use_stern_at_ic = (
   927	        stern_capacitance_model is not None
   928	        and float(stern_capacitance_model) > 0
   929	    )
   930	    if use_stern_at_ic:
   931	        stern_split_picard = {
   932	            "lambda_D": lambda_D,
   933	            "stern_coeff": float(stern_capacitance_model),
   934	            "eps": poisson_coefficient,
   935	        }
   936	    else:
   937	        stern_split_picard = None
   938	
   939	    # ----- Run shared scalar Picard outer loop -------------------------
   940	    # Generalized N-reaction loop with topology_hint dispatch.  See
   941	    # forms_logc.py counterpart and v3 §9 for the contract.
   942	    bulk_concs = [O_b, P_b, H_b]
   943	    diffusivities = [D_O, D_P, D_H]
   944	    species_floors = [1e-300, P_FLOOR, 1e-300]
   945	    ok, reason, picard_iters, picard_state = picard_outer_loop_general(
   946	        reactions=bv_reactions,
   947	        bulk_concs=bulk_concs,
   948	        diffusivities=diffusivities,
   949	        species_floors=species_floors,
   950	        h_idx=2,
   951	        c_clo4_bulk=c_clo4_bulk,
   952	        phi_applied_model=phi_applied_model,
   953	        bv_exp_scale=bv_exp_scale,
   954	        exponent_clip=exponent_clip,
   955	        clip_exponent=clip_exponent,
   956	        topology_hint=topology_hint_picard,
   957	        a_h=a_h_picard,
   958	        a_cl=a_cl_picard,
   959	        c_cl_anchor_kind=c_cl_anchor_kind,
   960	        stern_split=stern_split_picard,
   961	    )
   962	    ctx["initializer_picard_state"] = picard_state
   963	
   964	    if not ok:
   965	        return False, reason, picard_iters
   966	
   967	    R1 = picard_state["R1"]
   968	    R2 = picard_state["R2"]
   969	    O_s = picard_state["O_s"]
   970	    P_s = picard_state["P_s"]

   121	    """Assemble weak forms with the proton electrochemical-potential transform.
   122	
   123	    Primary unknowns: ``u_i = log(c_i)`` for non-mu species, ``mu_H =
   124	    u_H + em*z_H*phi`` for the proton, plus ``phi``.  Concentrations
   125	    reconstructed pointwise as

   858	    # ``psi_D`` is the post-Stern-split diffuse-layer drop, which the FE
   859	    # composite-psi profile picks up automatically (so phi(y=0) =
   860	    # phi_applied - psi_S after the IC interpolation).
   861	    stern_capacitance_model = scaling.get("bv_stern_capacitance_model")
   862	    use_stern_at_ic = (
   863	        stern_capacitance_model is not None
   864	        and float(stern_capacitance_model) > 0
   865	    )
   866	    if use_stern_at_ic:
   867	        stern_split_picard = {
   868	            "lambda_D": lambda_D,
   869	            "stern_coeff": float(stern_capacitance_model),
   870	            "eps": poisson_coefficient,
   871	        }
   872	    else:
   873	        stern_split_picard = None
   874	
   875	    # ----- Run shared scalar Picard outer loop -------------------------
   876	    # Generalized N-reaction loop with topology_hint dispatch.  For the
   877	    # sequential template (2 rxns, rxn1 produces H₂O₂, rxn2 consumes it,
   878	    # rxn2 irreversible) ``topology_hint='sequential_2e_h2o2'`` enables
   879	    # the legacy closed-form P_s/O_s reconstruction (byte-equivalent to
   880	    # the pre-M3a.3 2x2 ``picard_outer_loop`` for that topology).  All
   881	    # other topologies (parallel 2e/4e, future N-reaction sets) use the
   882	    # naive signed flux balance (v3 §2/§8).
   883	    bulk_concs = [O_b, P_b, H_b]
   884	    diffusivities = [D_O, D_P, D_H]
   885	    species_floors = [1e-300, P_FLOOR, 1e-300]
   886	    ok, reason, picard_iters, picard_state = picard_outer_loop_general(
   887	        reactions=bv_reactions,
   888	        bulk_concs=bulk_concs,
   889	        diffusivities=diffusivities,
   890	        species_floors=species_floors,
   891	        h_idx=2,
   892	        c_clo4_bulk=c_clo4_bulk,
   893	        phi_applied_model=phi_applied_model,
   894	        bv_exp_scale=bv_exp_scale,
   895	        exponent_clip=exponent_clip,
   896	        clip_exponent=clip_exponent,
   897	        a_h=a_h_picard,
   898	        a_cl=a_cl_picard,
   899	        c_cl_anchor_kind=c_cl_anchor_kind,
   900	        stern_split=stern_split_picard,
   901	        topology_hint=topology_hint_picard,
   902	    )
   903	    # Stash converged scalar state for downstream diagnostics
   904	    # (rate-consistency check; see scripts/diagnose_db_ic_distance.py
   905	    # and Codex's verification protocol in handoff #13 response).
   906	    ctx["initializer_picard_state"] = picard_state
   907	
   908	    if not ok:
   909	        return False, reason, picard_iters
   910

 succeeded in 0ms:
     1	"""Per-voltage diagnostics for the BV-PNP forward solver.
     2	
     3	Used by the C+D orchestrator and study scripts to capture failure-mode
     4	information (max phi, surface concentrations, SNES reason / iters,
     5	Bikerman steric saturation) without mutating the residual.
     6	
     7	The orchestrator stashes the active solver as ``ctx['_last_solver']`` in
     8	``_build_for_voltage`` so SNES diagnostics can be retrieved here without
     9	threading a solver argument through ``per_point_callback``.
    10	
    11	All routines treat missing ctx keys gracefully — diagnostics are
    12	best-effort, especially on the failure path where the orchestrator has
    13	already rolled back to the last accepted state.
    14	"""
    15	
    16	from __future__ import annotations
    17	
    18	import warnings
    19	from typing import Any, Optional
    20	
    21	import firedrake as fd
    22	import numpy as np
    23	
    24	from .config import _get_bv_boltzmann_counterions_cfg
    25	
    26	
    27	def surface_field_means(ctx: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, float]:
    28	    """Mean ``log(c_i)`` and ``c_i`` over the electrode boundary, plus phi.
    29	
    30	    Returns a flat dict with keys ``electrode_area_nondim``,
    31	    ``u{i}_surface_mean``, ``c{i}_surface_mean``, ``phi_surface_mean``,
    32	    plus ``mu{i}_surface_mean`` for any species treated as muh primary
    33	    variables (``i in ctx['mu_species']``).
    34	
    35	    For the production logc formulation, ``u{i}_surface_mean`` is the
    36	    surface mean of raw ``U.sub(i)`` (== ``u_i`` = ``log(c_i)``).
    37	
    38	    For the muh formulation (``ctx['logc_muh_transform']`` is True), the
    39	    surface mean of ``log(c_i)`` for the proton species is computed from
    40	    the muh-aware expression ``ctx['u_exprs'][i] = mu_H - em*z_H*phi``,
    41	    so ``u{i}_surface_mean`` is still semantically the surface mean of
    42	    ``log(c_i)`` -- the contract is consistent across formulations.
    43	    Additionally, ``mu{i}_surface_mean`` reports the surface mean of the
    44	    raw muh primary variable ``U.sub(i)``.
    45	
    46	    NB: ``c{i}_surface_mean = exp(u_mean)`` retains the existing
    47	    ``exp(mean(u))`` Jensen-fault for both formulations -- a separate
    48	    correctness fix is tracked.  Overflowing ``exp(u)`` values are
    49	    reported as ``float('inf')``.
    50	    """
    51	    bv_settings = ctx["bv_settings"]
    52	    elec_marker = int(bv_settings["electrode_marker"])
    53	    mesh = ctx["mesh"]
    54	    U = ctx["U"]
    55	    n = ctx["n_species"]
    56	
    57	    # Prefer ctx-stored log-c expressions when available (handles muh).
    58	    # Falls back to raw U.sub(i) for backwards compat with logc-only ctx.
    59	    u_exprs = ctx.get("u_exprs", None)
    60	    mu_species = frozenset(int(i) for i in ctx.get("mu_species", []))
    61	
    62	    ds_e = fd.ds(domain=mesh, subdomain_id=elec_marker)
    63	    area = float(fd.assemble(fd.Constant(1.0) * ds_e))
    64	    out: dict[str, float] = {"electrode_area_nondim": area}
    65	    if area <= 0:
    66	        return out
    67	
    68	    for i in range(n):
    69	        log_c_expr = u_exprs[i] if u_exprs is not None else U.sub(i)
    70	        u_mean = float(fd.assemble(log_c_expr * ds_e)) / area
    71	        out[f"u{i}_surface_mean"] = u_mean
    72	        try:
    73	            out[f"c{i}_surface_mean"] = float(np.exp(u_mean))
    74	        except OverflowError:
    75	            out[f"c{i}_surface_mean"] = float("inf")
    76	        if i in mu_species:
    77	            # Raw muh primary variable surface mean (offset from u_mean by em*z*phi_surf).
    78	            out[f"mu{i}_surface_mean"] = float(fd.assemble(U.sub(i) * ds_e)) / area
    79	    out["phi_surface_mean"] = float(fd.assemble(U.sub(n) * ds_e)) / area
    80	    return out
    81	
    82	
    83	def collect_diagnostics(
    84	    ctx: dict[str, Any],
    85	    *,
    86	    phase: str,
    87	    params: Optional[dict[str, Any]] = None,
    88	    picard_iters: Optional[int] = None,
    89	    steric_cap: float = 100.0,
    90	) -> dict[str, Any]:
    91	    """Assemble a per-voltage diagnostic record.
    92	
    93	    Parameters
    94	    ----------
    95	    phase:
    96	        Pipeline stage that produced the state, e.g. ``"cold_z_ramp"``,
    97	        ``"cold_no_z_ramp"``, ``"warm_walk"``, or ``"failed"``.
    98	    params:
    99	        Optional ``solver_params[10]`` dict.  When provided, analytic
   100	        Boltzmann counterions are parsed from ``params['bv_bc']`` and the
   101	        per-counterion surface concentration ``c_bulk · exp(-z·phi_surf)``
   102	        is computed.  When omitted, those fields are absent.
   103	    picard_iters:
   104	        Number of Picard iterations the analytical IC took, if
   105	        applicable.  ``None`` for the linear-phi initializer.
   106	    steric_cap:
   107	        Bikerman saturation threshold on Boltzmann counterion surface
   108	        concentration (nondim).
   109	    """
   110	    n = ctx["n_species"]
   111	    U = ctx["U"]
   112	    out: dict[str, Any] = {"phase": phase}
   113	
   114	    phi_data = U.dat[n].data_ro
   115	    out["max_phi"] = float(phi_data.max()) if phi_data.size else None
   116	    out["min_phi"] = float(phi_data.min()) if phi_data.size else None
   117	
   118	    # Per-volume min/max of log(c_i): for non-mu species this is raw
   119	    # U.dat[i] (== u_i); for mu species this is the muh-reconstructed
   120	    # log(c_i) = mu_H - em*z_H*phi at dofs.  Both formulations expose
   121	    # ``min_u{i}/max_u{i}`` consistently as log-concentration extremes.
   122	    # Additionally report ``min_mu{i}/max_mu{i}`` for muh species so the
   123	    # raw muh primary-variable extremes are observable.
   124	    em = float(ctx.get("nondim", {}).get("electromigration_prefactor", 1.0))
   125	    z_consts = ctx.get("z_consts", [])
   126	    mu_species = frozenset(int(i) for i in ctx.get("mu_species", []))
   127	
   128	    for i in range(n):
   129	        u_data_raw = U.dat[i].data_ro
   130	        if u_data_raw.size == 0:
   131	            continue
   132	        if i in mu_species:
   133	            try:
   134	                z_i = float(z_consts[i])
   135	            except (IndexError, TypeError):
   136	                z_i = 0.0
   137	            log_c_data = u_data_raw - em * z_i * phi_data
   138	            out[f"max_u{i}"] = float(log_c_data.max())
   139	            out[f"min_u{i}"] = float(log_c_data.min())
   140	            out[f"max_mu{i}"] = float(u_data_raw.max())
   141	            out[f"min_mu{i}"] = float(u_data_raw.min())
   142	        else:
   143	            out[f"max_u{i}"] = float(u_data_raw.max())
   144	            out[f"min_u{i}"] = float(u_data_raw.min())
   145	
   146	    try:
   147	        out.update(surface_field_means(ctx))
   148	    except Exception as exc:
   149	        out["surface_fields_error"] = f"{type(exc).__name__}: {exc}"
   150	
   151	    if params is not None:
   152	        try:
   153	            counterions = _get_bv_boltzmann_counterions_cfg(params)
   154	        except Exception:
   155	            counterions = []
   156	        phi_surf = out.get("phi_surface_mean")
   157	        if phi_surf is not None and counterions:
   158	            # For bikerman entries we need bulk dynamic packing
   159	            # ``A_dyn_bulk`` and the surface ``A_dyn_surf`` to evaluate
   160	            # the closure at the surface.  Pull from ctx when available
   161	            # (steric_a_funcs published by build_forms_logc); fall back
   162	            # to ``A_dyn_surf = A_dyn_bulk`` if the steric block was
   163	            # never built (purely-ideal config).
   164	            a_dyn_floats: list[float] = []
   165	            steric_a_funcs = ctx.get("steric_a_funcs") or []
   166	            for af in steric_a_funcs:
   167	                try:
   168	                    a_dyn_floats.append(float(af.dat.data_ro[0]))
   169	                except Exception:
   170	                    a_dyn_floats.append(0.0)
   171	            scaling = ctx.get("nondim", {}) or {}
   172	            c0_dyn = list(scaling.get("c0_model_vals", [])) or []
   173	            A_dyn_bulk = (
   174	                sum(a * c for a, c in zip(a_dyn_floats, c0_dyn[:len(a_dyn_floats)]))
   175	                if a_dyn_floats and c0_dyn else 0.0
   176	            )
   177	            # Surface A_dyn from the per-species c{i}_surface_mean already
   178	            # in `out` (populated by surface_field_means).
   179	            A_dyn_surf = 0.0
   180	            for i, a_i in enumerate(a_dyn_floats):
   181	                c_i_surf = out.get(f"c{i}_surface_mean")
   182	                if c_i_surf is None or not np.isfinite(c_i_surf):
   183	                    A_dyn_surf = A_dyn_bulk  # conservative fallback
   184	                    break
   185	                A_dyn_surf += a_i * float(c_i_surf)
   186	
   187	            within = True
   188	            for j, ci_spec in enumerate(counterions):
   189	                z = int(ci_spec["z"])
   190	                c_bulk = float(ci_spec["c_bulk_nondim"])
   191	                steric_mode = ci_spec.get("steric_mode", "ideal")
   192	                if steric_mode == "bikerman":
   193	                    a_b = float(ci_spec["a_nondim"])
   194	                    phi_clamp = float(ci_spec.get("phi_clamp", 50.0))
   195	                    theta_b = 1.0 - A_dyn_bulk - a_b * c_bulk
   196	                    if theta_b <= 0:
   197	                        c_surf = float("inf")
   198	                    else:
   199	                        phi_eff = max(-phi_clamp, min(phi_clamp, float(phi_surf)))
   200	                        try:
   201	                            q = float(np.exp(-z * phi_eff))
   202	                        except OverflowError:
   203	                            q = float("inf")
   204	                        free_dyn = max(1.0 - A_dyn_surf, 1e-10)
   205	                        denom = theta_b + a_b * c_bulk * q
   206	                        c_surf = (
   207	                            c_bulk * q * free_dyn / denom
   208	                            if np.isfinite(q) else (1.0 - A_dyn_surf) / a_b
   209	                        )
   210	                else:
   211	                    try:
   212	                        c_surf = c_bulk * float(np.exp(-z * phi_surf))
   213	                    except OverflowError:
   214	                        c_surf = float("inf")
   215	                out[f"c_counterion{j}_surface_mean"] = c_surf
   216	                out[f"c_counterion{j}_z"] = z
   217	                out[f"c_counterion{j}_steric_mode"] = steric_mode
   218	                if not (c_surf <= steric_cap):
   219	                    within = False
   220	            out["surface_counterion_within_steric"] = within
   221	
   222	    out["picard_iters"] = picard_iters
   223	    out["initializer_fallback"] = bool(ctx.get("initializer_fallback", False))
   224	
   225	    solver = ctx.get("_last_solver")
   226	    if solver is not None:
   227	        try:
   228	            out["snes_reason"] = str(solver.snes.getConvergedReason())
   229	            out["snes_iters"] = int(solver.snes.getIterationNumber())
   230	        except Exception as exc:

exec

   613	def set_initial_conditions_logc_muh(ctx: dict[str, Any], solver_params: Any) -> None:
   614	    """Linear-phi IC for the muh formulation.
   615	
   616	    Sets:
   617	
   618	      non-mu species:   u_i(y) = ln(c0_i)              (constant, same as logc)
   619	      mu species:       mu_H(y) = ln(c0_H) + em*z_H*phi_init(y)
   620	      phi:              phi_init(y) = phi_surface * (1 - y)
   621	
   622	    Pointwise reconstruction of c_H from these IC fields recovers
   623	    c_H_bulk exactly when phi_o_bulk = 0:
   624	
   625	      exp(mu_H(y) - em*z_H*phi(y)) = c_H_bulk * exp(-em*z_H*(phi(y) - phi_init(y)))
   626	
   627	    For Stern-aware configs, ``phi_surface = phi_applied - psi_S``
   628	    instead of ``phi_applied`` (Phase F fix; see forms_logc.py
   629	    counterpart for full rationale).
   630	    """
   631	    from .picard_ic import solve_stern_split
   632	
   633	    try:
   634	        n_species, order, dt, t_end, z_vals, D_vals, a_vals, phi_applied, c0, phi0, params = solver_params
   635	    except Exception as exc:
   636	        raise ValueError("bv_solver expects a list of 11 solver parameters") from exc
   637	
   638	    mesh = ctx["mesh"]
   639	    U_prev = ctx["U_prev"]
   640	    n = ctx["n_species"]
   641	    scaling = ctx.get("nondim", {})
   642	
   643	    c0_raw = [float(v) for v in ([c0] * n if np.isscalar(c0) else list(c0))][:n]
   644	    c0_model = scaling.get("c0_model_vals", c0_raw)
   645	    phi_applied_model = scaling.get("phi_applied_model", float(phi_applied))
   646	    em = float(scaling.get("electromigration_prefactor", 1.0))
   647	
   648	    mu_h_idx = _resolve_mu_h_index(list(z_vals))
   649	    mu_species = {mu_h_idx}
   650	
   651	    # Stern-aware anchoring (Phase F).
   652	    stern_capacitance_model = scaling.get("bv_stern_capacitance_model")
   653	    use_stern_at_ic = (
   654	        stern_capacitance_model is not None
   655	        and float(stern_capacitance_model) > 0
   656	    )
   657	    phi_surface = float(phi_applied_model)
   658	    if use_stern_at_ic and n >= 3 and len(c0_model) >= 3:
   659	        counterions = _get_bv_boltzmann_counterions_cfg(params)
   660	        c_clo4_bulk = None
   661	        a_cl_bulk = 0.0
   662	        if counterions:
   663	            c_clo4_bulk = max(float(counterions[0]["c_bulk_nondim"]), 1e-300)
   664	            for e in counterions:
   665	                if e.get("steric_mode", "ideal") == "bikerman":
   666	                    a_cl_bulk = float(e.get("a_nondim", 0.0))
   667	                    break
   668	        elif n == 4 and len(c0_model) >= 4:
   669	            c_clo4_bulk = max(float(c0_model[3]), 1e-300)
   670	            a_vals_full = list(solver_params[6])
   671	            if len(a_vals_full) >= 4:
   672	                a_cl_bulk = float(a_vals_full[3])
   673	        if c_clo4_bulk is not None:
   674	            H_b = max(float(c0_model[2]), 1e-300)
   675	            phi_o_bulk = math.log(H_b / c_clo4_bulk)
   676	            poisson_coefficient = float(scaling.get("poisson_coefficient", 1.0))
   677	            lambda_D_bulk = math.sqrt(max(poisson_coefficient, 1e-300))
   678	            _, _, phi_surface = solve_stern_split(
   679	                phi_applied_model=float(phi_applied_model),
   680	                phi_o=phi_o_bulk,
   681	                lambda_D=lambda_D_bulk,
   682	                c_clo4_bulk=c_clo4_bulk,
   683	                a_cl=a_cl_bulk,
   684	                stern_coeff_nondim=float(stern_capacitance_model),
   685	                eps_nondim=poisson_coefficient,
   686	            )
   687	
   688	    coords = fd.SpatialCoordinate(mesh)
   689	    ndim = mesh.geometric_dimension()
   690	    if ndim == 1:
   691	        spatial_var = coords[0]
   692	    else:
   693	        spatial_var = coords[1]
   694	
   695	    phi_init_expr = fd.Constant(phi_surface) * (1.0 - spatial_var)
   696	
   697	    _C_FLOOR = 1e-20
   698	    for i in range(n):
   699	        c0_i = max(float(c0_model[i]), _C_FLOOR)
   700	        if i in mu_species:
   701	            # mu_H_init(y) = ln(c0_H) + em*z_H*phi_init(y)
   702	            # -> reconstructs c_H = c0_H pointwise (when bulk phi=0).
   703	            U_prev.sub(i).interpolate(
   704	                fd.Constant(np.log(c0_i))
   705	                + fd.Constant(em * float(z_vals[i])) * phi_init_expr
   706	            )
   707	        else:
   708	            U_prev.sub(i).assign(fd.Constant(np.log(c0_i)))
   709	
   710	    U_prev.sub(n).interpolate(phi_init_expr)
   711	    ctx["U"].assign(U_prev)
   712	
   713	
   714	def set_initial_conditions_debye_boltzmann_logc_muh(
   715	    ctx: dict[str, Any], solver_params: Any
   716	) -> None:
   717	    """Matched-asymptotic IC for the muh stack at high anodic phi.
   718	
   719	    Identical Picard outer loop + Gouy-Chapman analytical Debye layer to
   720	    the logc variant (``set_initial_conditions_debye_boltzmann_logc``);
   721	    the only difference is the assignment for the proton species, which
   722	    writes the muh primary variable
   723	
   724	        mu_H_init(y) = u_H_init(y) + em*z_H*phi_init(y)
   725	
   726	    With the production scaling ``em*z_H = 1`` the Debye-layer ``psi``
   727	    cancels analytically (Boltzmann equilibrium), so ``mu_H_init`` reduces
   728	    to ``2*log(H_outer) - log(c_clo4_bulk)``  -- exactly the smooth
   729	    initial variable Newton wants in the diffuse layer.
   730	
   731	    On Picard non-convergence or a degenerate config falls back to the
   732	    muh linear-phi IC and sets ``ctx['initializer_fallback']=True``.
   733	
   734	    Wraps the body in ``firedrake.adjoint.stop_annotating()`` so the
   735	    Picard iterations and IC interpolations do not reach the pyadjoint
   736	    tape.
   737	    """
   738	    import firedrake.adjoint as adj
   739	
   740	    try:
   741	        n_species, order, dt, t_end, z_vals, D_vals, a_vals, phi_applied, c0, phi0, params = solver_params
   742	    except Exception as exc:
   743	        raise ValueError("bv_solver expects a list of 11 solver parameters") from exc
   744	
   745	    with adj.stop_annotating():
   746	        ok, reason, picard_iters = _try_debye_boltzmann_ic_muh(
   747	            ctx, solver_params, params, phi_applied, c0, n_species
   748	        )
   749	        if ok:
   750	            ctx["initializer_fallback"] = False
   751	            ctx["initializer_picard_iters"] = picard_iters
   752	            return
   753	        ctx["initializer_fallback"] = True
   754	        ctx["initializer_fallback_reason"] = reason
   755	        ctx["initializer_picard_iters"] = picard_iters
   756	        set_initial_conditions_logc_muh(ctx, solver_params)
   757	
   758	
   759	def _try_debye_boltzmann_ic_muh(
   760	    ctx: dict[str, Any],

   556	def set_initial_conditions_logc(ctx: dict[str, Any], solver_params: Any) -> None:
   557	    """Set initial conditions in log-concentration space.
   558	
   559	    Sets u_i = ln(c0_i) for species, linear phi profile.
   560	
   561	    When the residual is Stern-aware, the linear phi anchors at the
   562	    OHP-side surface potential ``phi_applied - psi_S`` rather than
   563	    ``phi_applied`` -- otherwise every fallback row sees the residual
   564	    eta collapse to ``-E_eq`` (handoff #12 §6, Codex's Fix 3).
   565	    """
   566	    import math
   567	    from .picard_ic import solve_stern_split
   568	
   569	    try:
   570	        n_species, order, dt, t_end, z_vals, D_vals, a_vals, phi_applied, c0, phi0, params = solver_params
   571	    except Exception as exc:
   572	        raise ValueError("bv_solver expects a list of 11 solver parameters") from exc
   573	
   574	    mesh = ctx["mesh"]
   575	    U_prev = ctx["U_prev"]
   576	    n = ctx["n_species"]
   577	    scaling = ctx.get("nondim", {})
   578	
   579	    c0_raw = [float(v) for v in ([c0] * n if np.isscalar(c0) else list(c0))][:n]
   580	    c0_model = scaling.get("c0_model_vals", c0_raw)
   581	    phi_applied_model = scaling.get("phi_applied_model", float(phi_applied))
   582	
   583	    # Stern-aware anchoring (Phase F).  When use_stern is active, solve
   584	    # for ``psi_S`` at bulk outer values so the linear phi profile does
   585	    # not collapse to phi(0) = phi_applied (which would give residual
   586	    # eta = -E_eq for every fallback row).
   587	    stern_capacitance_model = scaling.get("bv_stern_capacitance_model")
   588	    use_stern_at_ic = (
   589	        stern_capacitance_model is not None
   590	        and float(stern_capacitance_model) > 0
   591	    )
   592	    phi_surface = phi_applied_model
   593	    if use_stern_at_ic and n >= 3 and len(c0_model) >= 3:
   594	        # Bulk outer reference: phi_o_bulk = log(H_b / c_clo4_bulk).
   595	        # Need a counterion bulk concentration estimate.  Pull from the
   596	        # config (analytic boltzmann_counterions or synthesised 4sp).
   597	        counterions = _get_bv_boltzmann_counterions_cfg(params)
   598	        c_clo4_bulk = None
   599	        a_cl_bulk = 0.0
   600	        if counterions:
   601	            c_clo4_bulk = max(float(counterions[0]["c_bulk_nondim"]), 1e-300)
   602	            for e in counterions:
   603	                if e.get("steric_mode", "ideal") == "bikerman":
   604	                    a_cl_bulk = float(e.get("a_nondim", 0.0))
   605	                    break
   606	        elif n == 4 and len(c0_model) >= 4:
   607	            c_clo4_bulk = max(float(c0_model[3]), 1e-300)
   608	            a_vals_full = list(solver_params[6])
   609	            if len(a_vals_full) >= 4:
   610	                a_cl_bulk = float(a_vals_full[3])
   611	        if c_clo4_bulk is not None:
   612	            H_b = max(float(c0_model[2]), 1e-300)
   613	            phi_o_bulk = math.log(H_b / c_clo4_bulk)
   614	            poisson_coefficient = float(scaling.get("poisson_coefficient", 1.0))
   615	            lambda_D_bulk = math.sqrt(max(poisson_coefficient, 1e-300))
   616	            psi_S, _, phi_surface_split = solve_stern_split(
   617	                phi_applied_model=float(phi_applied_model),
   618	                phi_o=phi_o_bulk,
   619	                lambda_D=lambda_D_bulk,
   620	                c_clo4_bulk=c_clo4_bulk,
   621	                a_cl=a_cl_bulk,
   622	                stern_coeff_nondim=float(stern_capacitance_model),
   623	                eps_nondim=poisson_coefficient,
   624	            )
   625	            phi_surface = phi_surface_split
   626	
   627	    coords = fd.SpatialCoordinate(mesh)
   628	    ndim = mesh.geometric_dimension()
   629	
   630	    _C_FLOOR = 1e-20
   631	    for i in range(n):
   632	        c0_i = max(float(c0_model[i]), _C_FLOOR)
   633	        U_prev.sub(i).assign(fd.Constant(np.log(c0_i)))
   634	
   635	    # Linear potential profile
   636	    if ndim == 1:
   637	        spatial_var = coords[0]
   638	    else:
   639	        spatial_var = coords[1]
   640	    U_prev.sub(n).interpolate(fd.Constant(float(phi_surface)) * (1.0 - spatial_var))
   641	    ctx["U"].assign(U_prev)
   642

   644	def set_initial_conditions_debye_boltzmann_logc(
   645	    ctx: dict[str, Any], solver_params: Any
   646	) -> None:
   647	    """Matched-asymptotic IC for the log-c stack at high anodic phi.
   648	
   649	    Outer ambipolar 2*D_H proton transport + 2x2 algebraic surface-rate
   650	    Picard solve + Gouy-Chapman analytical Debye layer.  Seeds Newton on
   651	    the depleted-H+ / enriched-counterion manifold so the solver does not
   652	    have to discover the O(40) Boltzmann depletion in a single step.
   653	    See ``docs/PNP_BV_Analytical_Simplifications.md``.
   654	
   655	    On Picard non-convergence (max iters, NaN, singular Jacobian), or on
   656	    a degenerate config (no Boltzmann counterion, n_species < 3), falls
   657	    back to the linear-phi IC and sets ``ctx['initializer_fallback']=True``
   658	    with a string in ``ctx['initializer_fallback_reason']``.
   659	
   660	    The whole body runs under ``firedrake.adjoint.stop_annotating()`` so
   661	    Picard iterations and IC interpolations never reach the pyadjoint tape
   662	    -- the IC is an initial guess, not a control.
   663	    """
   664	    import math
   665	    import firedrake.adjoint as adj
   666	
   667	    try:
   668	        n_species, order, dt, t_end, z_vals, D_vals, a_vals, phi_applied, c0, phi0, params = solver_params
   669	    except Exception as exc:
   670	        raise ValueError("bv_solver expects a list of 11 solver parameters") from exc
   671	
   672	    with adj.stop_annotating():
   673	        ok, reason, picard_iters = _try_debye_boltzmann_ic(
   674	            ctx, solver_params, params, phi_applied, c0, n_species
   675	        )
   676	        if ok:
   677	            ctx["initializer_fallback"] = False
   678	            ctx["initializer_picard_iters"] = picard_iters
   679	            return
   680	        ctx["initializer_fallback"] = True
   681	        ctx["initializer_fallback_reason"] = reason
   682	        ctx["initializer_picard_iters"] = picard_iters
   683	        set_initial_conditions_logc(ctx, solver_params)
   684	
   685	
   686	def _try_debye_boltzmann_ic(
   687	    ctx: dict[str, Any],
   688	    solver_params: Any,
   689	    params: Any,
   690	    phi_applied: float,
   691	    c0: Any,
   692	    n_species: int,
   693	) -> tuple[bool, str, int]:
   694	    """Picard + Gouy-Chapman IC body. Returns (success, reason, picard_iters).
   695	
   696	    Wraps the shared scalar Picard outer loop in
   697	    ``Forward.bv_solver.picard_ic.picard_outer_loop``.  This function
   698	    handles config unpacking, counterion detection, mesh / coordinate
   699	    setup, and the post-Picard FE interpolation (Bikerman composite-psi
   700	    + multispecies-gamma seed, or legacy ideal-counterion GC).  All

     1	"""Butler-Volmer BC PNP forward solver.
     2	
     3	The production stack is:
     4	
     5	  * **3 dynamic species** (O2, H2O2, H+) with **log-concentration primary
     6	    variables** ``u_i = ln(c_i)``: enforces positivity, removes the
     7	    surface-concentration clip in BV evaluation, extends the converged
     8	    voltage window.
     9	  * **Analytic Boltzmann counterion** for ClO4- in the Poisson residual
    10	    (Poisson-Boltzmann-Nernst-Planck reduction).
    11	  * **Log-rate Butler-Volmer**: eliminates phantom R2 sinks at high
    12	    anodic eta.
    13	
    14	The stack is selected through three config flags::
    15	
    16	    params['bv_convergence']['formulation'] = 'logc'
    17	    params['bv_convergence']['bv_log_rate'] = True
    18	    params['bv_bc']['boltzmann_counterions'] = [{...}]
    19	
    20	See ``writeups/WeekOfApr27/PNP Inverse Solver Revised.tex`` for the
    21	formulation rationale and ``docs/bv_solver_unified_api.md`` for usage.
    22	
    23	The canonical I-V driver is
    24	``solve_grid_per_voltage_cold_with_warm_fallback`` (C+D continuation
    25	orchestrator).
    26

/bin/zsh -lc "nl -ba Forward/bv_solver/dispatch.py | sed -n '1,130p'" in /Users/jakeweinstein/Desktop/ResearchForwardSolverClone/FireDrakeEnvCG/PNPInverse
 succeeded in 0ms:
     1	"""Formulation dispatcher for the BV-PNP forward solver.
     2	
     3	The production stack uses the log-concentration backend (``forms_logc``).
     4	An experimental proton-electrochemical-potential variant
     5	(``forms_logc_muh``) is available for ``formulation="logc_muh"``; the muh
     6	backend stores the proton primary variable as ``mu_H = u_H + em*z_H*phi``
     7	to give Newton a smoother variable in Debye-layer regions where ``u_H``
     8	and ``phi`` separately vary by tens of log-units.  See
     9	``Forward/bv_solver/forms_logc_muh.py`` for the math and
    10	``docs/electrochemical_potential_solver_plan.md`` for the landing plan.
    11	
    12	``build_context`` / ``build_forms`` / ``set_initial_conditions`` dispatch on:
    13	
    14	  - ``params['bv_convergence']['formulation']``  -- selects backend module
    15	    (``"logc"`` or ``"logc_muh"``).
    16	  - ``params['bv_convergence']['initializer']``  -- selects IC routine
    17	    within the chosen backend (``"linear_phi"`` or ``"debye_boltzmann"``).
    18	
    19	The ``*_logc`` and ``*_logc_muh`` names are re-exported for scripts that
    20	want to be explicit about the backend they target.
    21	"""
    22	
    23	from __future__ import annotations
    24	
    25	from typing import Any
    26	
    27	from .forms_logc import (
    28	    build_context_logc,
    29	    build_forms_logc,
    30	    set_initial_conditions_logc,
    31	    set_initial_conditions_debye_boltzmann_logc,
    32	)
    33	from .forms_logc_muh import (
    34	    build_context_logc_muh,
    35	    build_forms_logc_muh,
    36	    set_initial_conditions_logc_muh,
    37	    set_initial_conditions_debye_boltzmann_logc_muh,
    38	)
    39	
    40	
    41	def _read_bv_convergence_field(solver_params: Any, key: str, default: str) -> str:
    42	    """Read ``bv_convergence[key]`` with a graceful default.
    43	
    44	    Robust to ``SolverParams`` (via ``__getitem__``), legacy 11-tuples,
    45	    and malformed test inputs.  Falls back to ``default`` whenever the
    46	    config block is missing or non-dict.
    47	    """
    48	    try:
    49	        params_dict = solver_params[10] if hasattr(solver_params, "__getitem__") else None
    50	    except Exception:
    51	        params_dict = None
    52	    if not isinstance(params_dict, dict):
    53	        return default
    54	    bv_conv = params_dict.get("bv_convergence", {})
    55	    if not isinstance(bv_conv, dict):
    56	        return default
    57	    return str(bv_conv.get(key, default)).strip().lower()
    58	
    59	
    60	def _read_formulation(solver_params: Any) -> str:
    61	    return _read_bv_convergence_field(solver_params, "formulation", "logc")
    62	
    63	
    64	def _read_initializer(solver_params: Any) -> str:
    65	    return _read_bv_convergence_field(solver_params, "initializer", "linear_phi")
    66	
    67	
    68	def _resolve_backend(solver_params: Any) -> str:
    69	    """Pick a backend module name based on ``formulation``.
    70	
    71	    Returns one of ``"logc"`` or ``"logc_muh"``.  Unknown formulations
    72	    fall through to ``"logc"`` (the production default) -- the config
    73	    layer (``Forward/bv_solver/config.py:_validate_formulation``) already
    74	    rejects unknown names at parse time, so this is defensive only.
    75	    """
    76	    formulation = _read_formulation(solver_params)
    77	    if formulation == "logc_muh":
    78	        return "logc_muh"
    79	    return "logc"
    80	
    81	
    82	def build_context(solver_params: Any, *, mesh: Any = None) -> dict:
    83	    backend = _resolve_backend(solver_params)
    84	    if backend == "logc_muh":
    85	        return build_context_logc_muh(solver_params, mesh=mesh)
    86	    return build_context_logc(solver_params, mesh=mesh)
    87	
    88	
    89	def build_forms(ctx: dict, solver_params: Any) -> dict:
    90	    backend = _resolve_backend(solver_params)
    91	    if backend == "logc_muh":
    92	        return build_forms_logc_muh(ctx, solver_params)
    93	    return build_forms_logc(ctx, solver_params)
    94	
    95	
    96	def set_initial_conditions(
    97	    ctx: dict, solver_params: Any, *, blob: bool = False
    98	) -> None:
    99	    """Set initial conditions for the dispatched backend.
   100	
   101	    Dispatches on ``params['bv_convergence']['formulation']`` to pick the
   102	    backend, then on ``params['bv_convergence']['initializer']`` to pick
   103	    the IC routine within that backend:
   104	
   105	      - ``"linear_phi"``     -> ``set_initial_conditions_*``
   106	      - ``"debye_boltzmann"`` -> ``set_initial_conditions_debye_boltzmann_*``
   107	
   108	    ``blob`` is accepted for backward-compatible kwargs and silently
   109	    ignored -- blob ICs were a concentration-formulation feature removed
   110	    with that backend.
   111	    """
   112	    backend = _resolve_backend(solver_params)
   113	    initializer = _read_initializer(solver_params)
   114	    if backend == "logc_muh":
   115	        if initializer == "debye_boltzmann":
   116	            return set_initial_conditions_debye_boltzmann_logc_muh(ctx, solver_params)
   117	        return set_initial_conditions_logc_muh(ctx, solver_params)
   118	    if initializer == "debye_boltzmann":
   119	        return set_initial_conditions_debye_boltzmann_logc(ctx, solver_params)
   120	    return set_initial_conditions_logc(ctx, solver_params)
   121	
   122	
   123	__all__ = [
   124	    "build_context",
   125	    "build_forms",
   126	    "set_initial_conditions",
   127	    # logc backend (production)
   128	    "build_context_logc",
   129	    "build_forms_logc",
   130	    "set_initial_conditions_logc",

     8	    Phase 1 (C): per-voltage cold-start with internal z-ramp.

   230	        )

   232	        # robin_bc) so they don't pollute the PETSc options database with
   233	        # flattened "unknown option" warnings.

   236	        solve_opts = {k: v for k, v in _items if k not in _NON_PETSC_KEYS}

   239	        # silently accepts them, which would let a non-converged state

   251	    # ------------------------------------------------------------------
   252	    # SS time-stepping loop with SER adaptive dt
   253	    # ------------------------------------------------------------------
   254	    def _make_run_ss(ctx, solver, of_cd):
   255	        U = ctx["U"]
   256	        U_prev = ctx["U_prev"]
   257	        dt_const = ctx["dt_const"]
   258	        dt_max = float(dt_init) * float(dt_max_ratio)
   259	
   260	        def run_ss(max_steps: int) -> bool:
   261	            dt_val = float(dt_init)
   262	            dt_const.assign(dt_val)
   263	            prev_flux = None
   264	            prev_delta = None
   265	            steady_count = 0
   266	            for _ in range(1, max_steps + 1):
   267	                try:
   268	                    solver.solve()
   269	                except Exception:
   270	                    return False
   271	                U_prev.assign(U)
   272	                fv = float(fd.assemble(of_cd))
   273	                if prev_flux is not None:
   274	                    delta = abs(fv - prev_flux)
   275	                    sv = max(abs(fv), abs(prev_flux), ss_abs_tol)
   276	                    is_steady = (delta / sv <= ss_rel_tol) or (delta <= ss_abs_tol)
   277	                    steady_count = steady_count + 1 if is_steady else 0
   278	                    if prev_delta is not None and delta > 0:
   279	                        ratio = prev_delta / delta
   280	                        if ratio > 1.0:
   281	                            grow = min(ratio, dt_growth_cap)
   282	                            dt_val = min(dt_val * grow, dt_max)
   283	                        else:
   284	                            dt_val = max(dt_val * 0.5, float(dt_init))
   285	                        dt_const.assign(dt_val)
   286	                    prev_delta = delta
   287	                else:
   288	                    steady_count = 0
   289	                prev_flux = fv
   290	                if steady_count >= ss_consec:
   291	                    return True
   292	            return False
   293	
   294	        return run_ss

codex
The z-ramp failure is more damning than it first looks: at `z=0` the orchestrator has zeroed dynamic species charge and the shared Boltzmann z-scale, but BV kinetics and Stern are still full-strength. That means an ionic-strength ramp is probably not addressing the first hard failure mode.

 succeeded in 0ms:
   650	#     anodic constant, irreversible).
   651	#   - §4 affine matrix system M·R = b with per-species transport
   652	#     coefficient λ_i (1/D_i for ordinary species; 1/(2 D_H) for H⁺).
   653	#   - §7 outer Picard with explicit raw-vs-relaxed rate disambiguation
   654	#     (R_solve / R_old / R) and δ on the relaxed state.
   655	#   - §8 post-loop surface reconstruction with topology-hint dispatch
   656	#     (sequential closed-form P_s for "sequential_2e_h2o2"; naive flux
   657	#     balance otherwise).
   658	#   - §9 contract: legacy-compatible floors before failure classification;
   659	#     reject H⁺ as a linear substrate at adapter sites (item 11).
   660	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   661	
   662	def _eta_list_from_drop(
   663	    *,
   664	    eta_drop: float,
   665	    reactions: list,
   666	    bv_exp_scale: float,
   667	    exponent_clip: float,
   668	    clip_exponent: bool,
   669	) -> list[float]:
   670	    """Per-reaction clipped η vector ``η_j = clip(scale·(η_drop − E_j))``."""
   671	    return [
   672	        _eta_clipped(
   673	            eta_drop=eta_drop,
   674	            E=float(rxn.get("E_eq_model", 0.0)),
   675	            bv_exp_scale=bv_exp_scale,
   676	            exponent_clip=exponent_clip,
   677	            clip=clip_exponent,
   678	        )
   679	        for rxn in reactions
   680	    ]
   681	
   682	
   683	def _build_picard_prefactors(
   684	    *,
   685	    reactions: list,
   686	    log_gamma: float,
   687	    log_by_species: list[float],
   688	    eta_list: list[float],
   689	) -> tuple[list[float], list[float], list[float]]:
   690	    """Per-reaction ``(α̂_j, β̂_j, Ĉ_j)`` per derivation v3 §3.
   691	
   692	    Three-branch anodic dispatch:
   693	
   694	      - branch 1 (surface-species linear): ``reversible AND anodic_species
   695	        is not None`` → ``β̂_j ≠ 0``, ``Ĉ_j = 0``.
   696	      - branch 2 (affine constant): ``reversible AND anodic_species is
   697	        None AND c_ref_model > 1e-30`` → ``Ĉ_j ≠ 0``, ``β̂_j = 0``.
   698	      - branch 3 (irreversible): ``reversible == False`` (or both above
   699	        fail) → ``β̂_j = Ĉ_j = 0``.
   700	
   701	    γ-power: ``α̂_j ∝ γ^{1 + Σ_f power_f}``; ``β̂_j ∝ γ^1``;
   702	    ``Ĉ_j ∝ γ^0`` (residual does not multiply ``c_ref_model`` by activity).
   703	
   704	    Computed in log-space (mirrors ``picard_outer_loop`` line 481-487).
   705	    """
   706	    alpha_hat = []
   707	    beta_hat = []
   708	    c_hat = []
   709	    for j, rxn in enumerate(reactions):
   710	        k_j = float(rxn["k0_model"])
   711	        a_j = float(rxn["alpha"])
   712	        n_e_j = float(rxn["n_electrons"])
   713	        eta_j = eta_list[j]
   714	        factors_j = rxn.get("cathodic_conc_factors", [])
   715	        log_h_factor_j = _factor_log_from_species_logs(log_by_species, factors_j)
   716	        # α̂_j: cathodic prefactor with γ^{1 + Σ_f power_f} embedded via
   717	        # log_gamma + log_h_factor (which carries one log_gamma per H⁺
   718	        # power because log_by_species is γ-shifted).
   719	        log_alpha = (
   720	            math.log(max(k_j, 1e-300))
   721	            + log_gamma
   722	            + log_h_factor_j
   723	            - a_j * n_e_j * eta_j
   724	        )
   725	        alpha_hat.append(_safe_exp(log_alpha))
   726	
   727	        reversible = bool(rxn.get("reversible", False))
   728	        anod_sp = rxn.get("anodic_species", None)
   729	        c_ref = float(rxn.get("c_ref_model", 0.0))
   730	
   731	        if reversible and anod_sp is not None:
   732	            # Branch 1: surface-species linear (γ¹).
   733	            log_beta = (
   734	                math.log(max(k_j, 1e-300))
   735	                + log_gamma
   736	                + (1.0 - a_j) * n_e_j * eta_j
   737	            )
   738	            beta_hat.append(_safe_exp(log_beta))
   739	            c_hat.append(0.0)
   740	        elif reversible and anod_sp is None and c_ref > 1e-30:
   741	            # Branch 2: affine constant (γ⁰; no log_gamma).
   742	            log_c = (
   743	                math.log(max(k_j, 1e-300))
   744	                + math.log(max(c_ref, 1e-300))
   745	                + (1.0 - a_j) * n_e_j * eta_j
   746	            )
   747	            beta_hat.append(0.0)
   748	            c_hat.append(_safe_exp(log_c))
   749	        else:
   750	            # Branch 3: irreversible.
   751	            beta_hat.append(0.0)
   752	            c_hat.append(0.0)
   753	    return alpha_hat, beta_hat, c_hat
   754	
   755	
   756	def _lambda_for_species(
   757	    *, species_idx: int, h_idx: int, diffusivities: list[float]
   758	) -> float:
   759	    """``λ_i = 1/D_i`` for ordinary species; ``λ_H = 1/(2 D_H)`` for H⁺.
   760	
   761	    Per derivation v3 §4 sub-note + §9 contract item 11.  Adapter sites
   762	    must reject configs that put H⁺ as ``cathodic_species`` or
   763	    ``anodic_species`` BEFORE calling this function (this helper only
   764	    dispatches the divisor; it does not validate).
   765	    """
   766	    D_i = max(diffusivities[species_idx], 1e-30)
   767	    if species_idx == h_idx:
   768	        return 1.0 / (2.0 * D_i)
   769	    return 1.0 / D_i
   770	
   771	
   772	def _assemble_n_reaction_system(
   773	    *,
   774	    reactions: list,
   775	    alpha_hat: list[float],
   776	    beta_hat: list[float],
   777	    c_hat: list[float],
   778	    bulk_concs: list[float],
   779	    diffusivities: list[float],
   780	    h_idx: int,
   781	):
   782	    """Assemble M (N×N) and b (N) per derivation v3 §4.
   783	
   784	    ``M[j,k] = δ_{j,k} − α̂_j · s_{cathsub_j, k} · λ_{cathsub_j}
   785	              + β̂_j · s_{anodsub_j, k} · λ_{anodsub_j}``  (β̂_j=0 ⇒ second
   786	              term gone)
   787	
   788	    ``b[j] = α̂_j · c_{cathsub_j}_b − β̂_j · c_{anodsub_j}_b − Ĉ_j``
   789	
   790	    where ``λ_i = 1/D_i`` for ordinary species and ``1/(2 D_H)`` for H⁺
   791	    (substrate, not the H⁺ flux balance which doesn't enter M).
   792	
   793	    Returns ``(M, b)`` as lists-of-lists / list (so the caller can
   794	    convert to numpy arrays for the linear solve, keeping this helper
   795	    importable without numpy at module load).
   796	    """
   797	    N = len(reactions)
   798	    # Initialize M = identity, b = zeros.
   799	    M = [[(1.0 if j == k else 0.0) for k in range(N)] for j in range(N)]
   800	    b = [0.0 for _ in range(N)]
   801	    for j, rxn_j in enumerate(reactions):
   802	        # Disabled rxns get a trivial row M[j,j]=1, b[j]=0 ⇒ R_j=0.
   803	        # Avoids accumulating numerically-tiny alpha_hat[j] (from k0=0
   804	        # short-circuited to 1e-300 in _build_picard_prefactors) into M
   805	        # off-diagonals where it could amplify in poorly-conditioned
   806	        # matrices.  Topology classification is unaffected — the row
   807	        # exists, R_j is just identically zero.
   808	        if _is_reaction_disabled(rxn_j):
   809	            continue
   810	        cs = int(rxn_j["cathodic_species"])
   811	        lambda_cs = _lambda_for_species(
   812	            species_idx=cs, h_idx=h_idx, diffusivities=diffusivities
   813	        )
   814	        c_cs_b = float(bulk_concs[cs])
   815	        for k, rxn_k in enumerate(reactions):
   816	            stoich_k = list(rxn_k.get("stoichiometry", []))
   817	            if cs >= len(stoich_k):
   818	                continue
   819	            s_cs_k = float(stoich_k[cs])
   820	            if s_cs_k == 0.0:
   821	                continue
   822	            M[j][k] -= alpha_hat[j] * s_cs_k * lambda_cs
   823	        b[j] += alpha_hat[j] * c_cs_b
   824	
   825	        if beta_hat[j] != 0.0:
   826	            anod = rxn_j.get("anodic_species", None)
   827	            if anod is not None:
   828	                anod = int(anod)
   829	                lambda_as = _lambda_for_species(
   830	                    species_idx=anod, h_idx=h_idx, diffusivities=diffusivities
   831	                )
   832	                c_as_b = float(bulk_concs[anod])
   833	                for k, rxn_k in enumerate(reactions):
   834	                    stoich_k = list(rxn_k.get("stoichiometry", []))
   835	                    if anod >= len(stoich_k):
   836	                        continue
   837	                    s_as_k = float(stoich_k[anod])
   838	                    if s_as_k == 0.0:
   839	                        continue
   840	                    M[j][k] += beta_hat[j] * s_as_k * lambda_as
   841	                b[j] -= beta_hat[j] * c_as_b
   842	
   843	        b[j] -= c_hat[j]
   844	    return M, b
   845	
   846	
   847	def _solve_2x2(M: list, b: list) -> tuple[float, float, float]:
   848	    """Direct 2×2 solve preserving legacy ordering for byte-equivalence.
   849	
   850	    Returns ``(R0, R1, det)``.  Caller checks ``det`` for singularity.
   851	    Mirrors ``picard_outer_loop`` lines 496-502.
   852	    """
   853	    m11, m12 = M[0][0], M[0][1]
   854	    m21, m22 = M[1][0], M[1][1]
   855	    rhs1, rhs2 = b[0], b[1]
